Authorizer implementation starts loading its metadata.</li>\n    51→ *   <li>Broker starts SocketServer to accept connections and process requests.</li>\n    52→ *   <li>For each listener, SocketServer waits for authorization metadata to be available in the\n    53→ *       authorizer before accepting connections. The future returned by {@link #start(AuthorizerServerInfo)}\n    54→ *       for each listener must return only when authorizer is ready to authorize requests on the listener.</li>\n    55→ *   <li>Broker accepts connections. For each connection, broker performs authentication and then accepts Kafka requests.\n    56→ *       For each request, broker invokes {@link #authorize(AuthorizableRequestContext, List)} to authorize\n    57→ *       actions performed by the request.</li>\n    58→ * </ol>\n    59→ *\n    60→ * Authorizer implementation class may optionally implement @{@link org.apache.kafka.common.Reconfigurable}\n    61→ * to enable dynamic reconfiguration without restarting the broker.\n    62→ * <p>Authorizer implementation class may also optionally implement {@link org.apache.kafka.common.metrics.Monitorable}\n    63→ * to enable the authorizer to register metrics. The following tags are automatically added to all metrics registered:\n    64→ * <code>config</code> set to <code>authorizer.class.name</code>, <code>class</code> set to the Authorizer class name,\n    65→ * and <code>role</code> set to either <code>broker</code> or <code>controller</code>.\n    66→ * <p>\n    67→ * <b>Threading model:</b>\n    68→ * <ul>\n    69→ *   <li>All authorizer operations including authorization and ACL updates must be thread-safe.</li>\n    70→ *   <li>ACL update methods are asynchronous. Implementations with low update latency may return a\n    71→ *       completed future using {@link java.util.concurrent.CompletableFuture#completedFuture(Object)}.\n    72→ *       This ensures that the request will be handled synchronously by the caller without using a\n    73→ *       purgatory to wait for the result. If ACL updates require remote communication which may block,\n    74→ *       return a future that is completed asynchronously when the remote operation completes. This enables\n    75→ *       the caller to process other requests on the request threads without blocking.</li>\n    76→ *   <li>Any threads or thread pools used for processing remote operations asynchronously can be started during\n    77→ *       {@link #start(AuthorizerServerInfo)}. These threads must be shutdown during {@link Authorizer#close()}.</li>\n    78→ * </ul>\n    79→ * </p>\n    80→ */\n    81→public interface Authorizer extends Configurable, Closeable {\n    82→\n    83→    /**\n    84→     * Starts loading authorization metadata and returns futures that can be used to wait until\n    85→     * metadata for authorizing requests on each listener is available. Each listener will be\n    86→     * started only after its metadata is available and authorizer is ready to start authorizing\n    87→     * requests on that listener.\n    88→     *\n    89→     * @param serverInfo Metadata for the broker including broker id and listener endpoints\n    90→     * @return CompletionStage for each endpoint that completes when authorizer is ready to\n    91→     *         start authorizing requests on that listener.\n    92→     */\n    93→    Map<Endpoint, ? extends CompletionStage<Void>> start(AuthorizerServerInfo serverInfo);\n    94→\n    95→    /**\n    96→     * Authorizes the specified action. Additional metadata for the action is specified\n    97→     * in `requestContext`.\n    98→     * <p>\n    99→     * This is a synchronous API designed for use with locally cached ACLs. Since this method is invoked on the\n   100→     * request thread while processing each request, implementations of this method should avoid time-consuming\n   101→     * remote communication that may block request threads.\n   102→     *\n   103→     * @param requestContext Request context including request type, security protocol and listener name\n   104→     * @param actions Actions being authorized including resource and operation for each action\n   105→     * @return List of authorization results for each action in the same order as the provided actions\n   106→     */\n   107→    List<AuthorizationResult> authorize(AuthorizableRequestContext requestContext, List<Action> actions);\n   108→\n   109→    /**\n   110→     * Creates new ACL bindings.\n   111→     * <p>\n   112→     * This is an asynchronous API that enables the caller to avoid blocking during the update. Implementations of this\n   113→     * API can return completed futures using {@link java.util.concurrent.CompletableFuture#completedFuture(Object)}\n   114→     * to process the update synchronously on the request thread.\n   115→     *\n   116→     * @param requestContext Request context if the ACL is being created by a broker to handle\n   117→     *        a client request to create ACLs.\n   118→     * @param aclBindings ACL bindings to create\n   119→     *\n   120→     * @return Create result for each ACL binding in the same order as in the input list. Authorizer implementation starts loading its metadata.</li>\n *   <li>Broker starts SocketServer to accept connections and process requests.</li>\n *   <li>For each listener, SocketServer waits for authorization metadata to be available in the\n *       authorizer before accepting connections. The future returned by {@link #start(AuthorizerServerInfo)}\n *       for each listener must return only when authorizer is ready to authorize requests on the listener.</li>\n *   <li>Broker accepts connections. For each connection, broker performs authentication and then accepts Kafka requests.\n *       For each request, broker invokes {@link #authorize(AuthorizableRequestContext, List)} to authorize\n *       actions performed by the request.</li>\n * </ol>\n *\n * Authorizer implementation class may optionally implement @{@link org.apache.kafka.common.Reconfigurable}\n * to enable dynamic reconfiguration without restarting the broker.\n * <p>Authorizer implementation class may also optionally implement {@link org.apache.kafka.common.metrics.Monitorable}\n * to enable the authorizer to register metrics. The following tags are automatically added to all metrics registered:\n * <code>config</code> set to <code>authorizer.class.name</code>, <code>class</code> set to the Authorizer class name,\n * and <code>role</code> set to either <code>broker</code> or <code>controller</code>.\n * <p>\n * <b>Threading model:</b>\n * <ul>\n *   <li>All authorizer operations including authorization and ACL updates must be thread-safe.</li>\n *   <li>ACL update methods are asynchronous. Implementations with low update latency may return a\n *       completed future using {@link java.util.concurrent.CompletableFuture#completedFuture(Object)}.\n *       This ensures that the request will be handled synchronously by the caller without using a\n *       purgatory to wait for the result. If ACL updates require remote communication which may block,\n *       return a future that is completed asynchronously when the remote operation completes. This enables\n *       the caller to process other requests on the request threads without blocking.</li>\n *   <li>Any threads or thread pools used for processing remote operations asynchronously can be started during\n *       {@link #start(AuthorizerServerInfo)}. These threads must be shutdown during {@link Authorizer#close()}.</li>\n * </ul>\n * </p>\n */\npublic interface Authorizer extends Configurable, Closeable {\n\n    /**\n     * Starts loading authorization metadata and returns futures that can be used to wait until\n     * metadata for authorizing requests on each listener is available. DENY ACLs.\n        if (authorize(requestContext, Collections.singletonList(new Action(\n                op, new ResourcePattern(resourceType, \"hardcode\", PatternType.LITERAL),\n                0, EnumMap<PatternType, Set<String>> allowPatterns =\n            new EnumMap<>(PatternType.class) {{\n                    put(PatternType.LITERAL, new HashSet<>());\n requestContext.principal().getPrincipalType(),\n            requestContext.principal().getName());\n        String hostAddr = requestContext.clientAddress().getHostAddress();\n\n        for denyPatterns.get(PatternType.PREFIXED).add(binding.pattern().name());\n                        break;\n                    default:\n                }\n                continue;\n            }\n\n           allowPatterns.get(PatternType.LITERAL).add(binding.pattern().name());\n                    break;\n                case PREFIXED:\n                    allowPatterns.get(PatternType.PREFIXED).add(binding.pattern().name());\n                    break;\n                default:\n            }\n        }\n\n        if (hasWildCardAllow) {\n (denyPatterns.get(PatternType.PREFIXED).contains(sb.toString())) {\n                        hasDominatedDeny = true;\n                        break;\n                    }\n                }\n
